This first release supports the following 8 Indic languages:\r\n\r\n1.\tGujarati female and male voices\r\n2.\tHindi male voice (primarily for Windows 7 users)\r\n3.\tKannada female and male voice\r\n4.\tMarathi male voice\r\n5.\tPunjabi female voice\r\n6.\tSanskrit male voice\r\n7.\tTamil male voice\r\n8.\tTelugu female and male voices\r\n\r\nAfter successful installation of Indic Text To Speech (TTS) App, the installer creates a shortcut for the App on the Desktop.\r\n\r\nThe App User Interface lists the Hear2Read voices installed in the PC. The basic App incudes a English voice. There are two buttons at the bottom of the App window:\r\n\r\n-\tClicking the left button (Listen to a Demo Here) opens a browser window with Hear2Read.org demo. The user can select a voice and listen to TTS output for the selected voice.\r\n\r\n-\tClicking the right button (Get More Voices Here) opens the voice download page on Hear2Read web site where the user can download additional voices. \r\n\r\nAfter adding the voice, the Screen Reading App settings need to be changed to use the Voice as described in the User Guide for the Screen Reading App.\r\n\r\nMost of the TTS applications listed above provide the option to save speech output in an audio file.\r\n\r\nThis App can be used by people who cannot read printed text but understand the spoken language well.\r\n\r\nIt can be used to reduce the load of books that children have to carry to school, as a suitably formatted EBook and this App can replace the printed book.\r\n\r\nPlease
